processes and analyses new information words grammatical structures and and binds together with information already stored long term memory research suggests that people vary widely the amount information they can hold accessible namely working memory capacity negatively affecting their performance diverse cognitive tasks the field second language acquisition limited working memory capacity may result the inability integrate information find pronoun referent monitor for semantic inconsistencies between texts resolve lexical ambiguity abstract main theme make comparisons and perform well general comprehension daneman merickle bearing mind these implications and after conducting extensive studies researchers have put forward series strategies enhance learning children with working memory problems gathercole alloway recommend adapting the learning environment reducir memory loads the classroom target and train memory function directly either way the ultimate goal minimize the chances failure and enhance learning this claim supported series studies and case studies which students who received working memory training displayed noticeable improvement their recall capacity and attention general the basis this evidence this case study will focus the application number working memory boosting strategies improve second language students performance the population will consist low performance language students english foreign language from second fourth and sixth semester the english and french program universidad nariño who will given set out class activities and will
